This series along with the Braun Activator has now been discontinued. I have the Braun 360 Complete 8985 shaver. If someone can recall the Braun 360 was a minor upgrade to the Braun Activator line of shavers. The upgrade was in the foil and the cutter block assembly only. According to Braun, the newer cutter block and foil were better at cutting than the previous Activator series cutter block. Also the newer cutter block fit both Braun 360 complete as well as Braun Activator shavers.<br /><br />Braun has now discontinued the individual cutter blocks for these shavers and now they offer only the Braun Series 5 Combi 51S for both shavers. So, here's the deal:<br /><br />>>If you are looking for an exact replacement for the Braun 360 Complete line of shavers, then this Braun Series 5 Combi 51S is the right product for you. It is identical to the one you previously had except that 360 complete is not written on it.<br /><br />>>If you are looking for an exact replacement for the Braun Activator line of shavers then this is NOT the replacement for you. This will fit your shaver but it is a different product. You will be better served by getting the Braun Series 3 Combi 30B.<br /><br />Now for the quality of this cutter block and foil. It cuts like the original. Since I never had another shaver or another cutter block, so I cannot compare it to another. My original foil that came with the shaver got chipped within 4 months. I was quite upset but went ahead and bought another one, the replacement lasted for almost 3 years. So, now I have bought this one, let's hope this lasts for 3 years too. I have been using it for a month. This is made in Germany.   144. I won't bother reviewing the overall performance of the razors themselves for which this is a replacement. Presumably if you're in the market for one of these it's a bit too late for that. So, I will just address the issue of whether or not you should bother buying this replacement. Does it make sense to replace the cutter head as often as the manufacturer states, or even at all? I can unequivocally verify that Braun is not exaggerating when they claim the cutter blocks wear out after a year and a half. I don't know how the heck they quantitatively compute a percentage increase for the efficacy of a shave (25% better?), but qualitatively there is a huge difference.<br /><br />You probably think your razor hasn't deteriorated over the year and a half, but it has. You just don't notice it because it's gradual. However, when you put a new cutter in, the difference is dramatic. The shave pulls much less, and is much smoother.<br /><br />You can argue it's a bit unfortunate that the Braun cutter blocks don't last longer. I tend to agree. But the truth is they don't. This is especially true once they went to the Gillette-made cutter (with the beveled cutting surfaces). If anything, I'd recommend replacement once a year.

  581. This is the first time in a couple of years that I bought a cutter block & foil for my Braun 8585 Razor, and they definitely changed the design for the better. The foil is a more complex (usable) pattern and the center (whisker) cutters are larger and work better. But it's the cutter block that's undergone the most changes and which really help. Instead of the blades pointing up (which tends to dull them faster in any razor), they are now pointed to the sides...where each blade piece has to two ends. Which not only works better, but keeps the blades sharper (and hopefully longer). And it's also the first cutter block I've purchased in quite a while that was so well balanced, that the noise level of my razor went down quite a bit. In the past, buying a new cutter block never really helped much, and so I only bought the combination when the foil failed. And generally I could hardly tell the diference with the new combo. But not this time. This time it was very noticeable better.<br /><br />Not sure how long it will last, but I very much like the results of the design changes.

  956. In my experience the foil design of the 30b is FAR superior to the foil design of the 51s. The larger hexagon shaped holes in the 51s seem to allow a little &#34;wiggle' in the hair shaft as the block is cutting it, thereby creating a tugging/pulling force on the hair rather than cleanly shearing it. For me, the foil pattern on the 30b does a MUCH better job holding/stabilizing the hair so the block/blade below can make a clean cut without any tugging/pulling. Of course, this problem becomes more and more noticeable with longer intervals between shaving and/or as the blade edges deteriorate over time. If you're a daily shaver and/or change the block/foil frequently there's probably no discernible difference between the two but for anyone who, like me, goes a couple days between shaving and/or likes to maximize the life of the blade then the 30b is superior.
  957. Foil and cutter hard to find a good one for this razor, but this works great. Shaves good, cleans good, wish I had purcased more of them, hope they still have some when I go to reorder.
